#!/usr/bin/python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

from base64 import b64encode
from inspect import getsource, getmodule, currentframe

print(getsource(getmodule(currentframe())))

inp = input('>>> ')

if eval(b64encode(inp.encode())) == 1337:
    print(open('flag.txt').read())



>>> Traceback (most recent call last):
  File "/home/pwn/./pwn", line 11, in <module>
    if eval(b64encode(inp.encode())) == 1337:
       ^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^
  File "<string>", line 1
    MA==
SyntaxError: invalid syntax

from base64 import b64encode
from inspect import getsource, getmodule, currentframe

print(getsource(getmodule(currentframe())))

inp = input('>>> ')

if eval(b64encode(inp.encode())) == 1337:
    print(open('flag.txt').read())



>>> Traceback (most recent call last):
  File "/home/pwn/./pwn", line 11, in <module>
    if eval(b64encode(inp.encode())) == 1337:
       ^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^
  File "<string>", line 1, in <module>
NameError: name 'MTAw' is not defined

from inspect import getsource, getmodule, currentframe

print(getsource(getmodule(currentframe())))

inp = input('>>> ')

if eval(b64encode(inp.encode())) == 1337:
    print(open('flag.txt').read())



>>> Traceback (most recent call last):
  File "/home/pwn/./pwn", line 11, in <module>
    if eval(b64encode(inp.encode())) == 1337:
       ^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^
  File "<string>", line 1, in <module>
NameError: name 'MjAw' is not defined

# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

from base64 import b64encode
from inspect import getsource, getmodule, currentframe

print(getsource(getmodule(currentframe())))

inp = input('>>> ')

if eval(b64encode(inp.encode())) == 1337:
    print(open('flag.txt').read())

from inspect import getsource, getmodule, currentframe

print(getsource(getmodule(currentframe())))

inp = input('>>> ')

if eval(b64encode(inp.encode())) == 1337:
    print(open('flag.txt').read())



>>> Traceback (most recent call last):
  File "/home/pwn/./pwn", line 11, in <module>
    if eval(b64encode(inp.encode())) == 1337:
       ^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^
  File "<string>", line 1, in <module>

#!/usr/bin/python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

from base64 import b64encode
from inspect import getsource, getmodule, currentframe

print(getsource(getmodule(currentframe())))

inp = input('>>> ')

if eval(b64encode(inp.encode())) == 1337:
    print(open('flag.txt').read())

print(getsource(getmodule(currentframe())))

inp = input('>>> ')

if eval(b64encode(inp.encode())) == 1337:
    print(open('flag.txt').read())

# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

from base64 import b64encode
from inspect import getsource, getmodule, currentframe

print(getsource(getmodule(currentframe())))

inp = input('>>> ')

if eval(b64encode(inp.encode())) == 1337:
    print(open('flag.txt').read())
